<p>Include this prompt in your AI assistant to guide consistent code generation for Astro + Prisma + Prisma Postgres projects.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>GitHub Copilot</strong>: Type <code>#&lt;filename&gt;</code> to reference the prompt file.</li>
<li><strong>Cursor</strong>: Use <code>@Files</code> and select your prompt file.</li>
<li><strong>Zed</strong>: Use <code>/file</code> followed by your prompt&#x27;s path.</li>
<li><strong>Windsurf</strong>: Use <code>@Files</code> and choose your prompt file from the list.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="prompt"><a data-card="" href="#prompt" class="peer">Prompt</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"># Specify the following for Cursor rules</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">description: Guidelines for writing Astro.js apps with Prisma Postgres</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">alwaysApply: false</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"># Bootstrap Astro app with Prisma Postgres</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Overview of implementing Prisma with Astro</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Install Prisma and required dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Initialize Prisma with custom output path</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Configure schema with correct provider</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create global Prisma client instance with Accelerate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use Prisma client in API routes with proper error handling</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## 🚨 CRITICAL INSTRUCTIONS FOR AI LANGUAGE MODELS 🚨</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">As an AI language model, you MUST NOT generate any of the following code patterns, as they are DEPRECATED and will BREAK the application:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER GENERATE THIS CODE - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">     // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER USE default import location - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;@prisma/client&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER CREATE CLIENT WITHOUT ACCELERATE - IT WILL BREAK IN PRODUCTION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Instead, you MUST ALWAYS generate ONLY this pattern:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ ALWAYS GENERATE THIS EXACT PATTERN</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ ALWAYS USE THIS IMPORT PATH</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../generated/prisma/client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { withAccelerate } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/extension-accelerate&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ ALWAYS CREATE CLIENT WITH ACCELERATE EXTENSION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  datasourceUrl: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">meta</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">withAccelerate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">())</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## ABSOLUTE REQUIREMENTS FOR AI CODE GENERATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use custom output: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output = &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use Accelerate extension with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`withAccelerate()`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> if using Prisma Postgres</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`lib/prisma.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as a global singleton instance</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST wrap all database calls in try-catch blocks</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST import from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;../generated/prisma/client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;@prisma/client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import.meta.env.DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in Astro (not </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`process.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST ALWAYS use the full </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> command with ALL flags: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init --db --output ../src/generated/prisma --generator-provider prisma-client`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT INSTALLATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Dev dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> tsx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --save-dev</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Production dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> @prisma/extension-accelerate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> @prisma/client</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT PRISMA INITIALIZATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma init --db --output ../src/generated/prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT SCHEMA CONFIGURATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   = &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">datasource db {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  url      = env(&quot;DATABASE_URL&quot;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model YourModel {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        Int      @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt DateTime @default(now())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT GLOBAL PRISMA CLIENT</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**src/lib/prisma.ts**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../generated/prisma/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { withAccelerate } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/extension-accelerate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  datasourceUrl: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">meta</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">withAccelerate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT API ROUTE IMPLEMENTATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">All API routes MUST follow this pattern with proper error handling:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { APIRoute } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;astro&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../../../lib/prisma&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> GET</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> APIRoute</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.yourModel.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">findMany</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Response</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">stringify</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(data), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      status: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">200</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      headers: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Content-Type&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;application/json&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Error:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, error);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Response</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">stringify</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ error: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Failed to fetch data&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      status: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">500</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      headers: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Content-Type&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;application/json&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">};</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> POST</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> APIRoute</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ({ </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">request</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> body</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> request.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">json</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // Validate required fields</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">body.requiredField) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Response</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">stringify</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ error: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Required field missing&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        status: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">400</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        headers: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Content-Type&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;application/json&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.yourModel.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">create</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      data: body,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Response</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">stringify</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(result), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      status: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">201</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      headers: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Content-Type&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;application/json&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Error:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, error);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Response</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">JSON</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">stringify</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ error: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Failed to create data&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }), {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      status: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">500</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      headers: { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Content-Type&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;application/json&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">};</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT USAGE IN ASTRO PAGES</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Server-side data fetching in Astro pages:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```astro</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">import prisma from &#x27;../lib/prisma&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">// Fetch data on the server</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">const data = await prisma.yourModel.findMany()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;html&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  &lt;body&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    {data.map(item =&gt; (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;div&gt;{item.name}&lt;/div&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ))}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  &lt;/body&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;/html&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## AI MODEL VERIFICATION STEPS</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Before generating any code, you MUST verify:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output = &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you importing from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;../generated/prisma/client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`withAccelerate()`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> extension? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you wrapping database operations in try-catch? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import.meta.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`process.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`--generator-provider prisma-client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (NOT </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgresql`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CONSEQUENCES OF INCORRECT IMPLEMENTATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">If you generate code using:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `prisma-client-js`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> provider</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Default import from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/client`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> PrismaClient without Accelerate extension</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Missing custom output path</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">The implementation will:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Break in production</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Cause connection pool exhaustion</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Fail to maintain proper database connections</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Result in import errors</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Cause performance issues</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## USEFUL COMMANDS</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma generate              # Regenerate client after schema changes</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma migrate dev --name X  # Create and apply migration</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma studio                # Open visual database editor</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npx prisma db push               # Push schema without migration</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## AI MODEL RESPONSE TEMPLATE</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">When asked about Prisma + Astro implementation, you MUST:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ONLY use code from this guide</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER suggest deprecated approaches</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS use the exact patterns shown above</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> VERIFY your response against the patterns shown here</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS include error handling in API routes</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS use the global prisma instance from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`lib/prisma.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Remember: There are NO EXCEPTIONS to these rules.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="running-the-application"><a data-card="" href="#running-the-application" class="peer">Running the application</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Get your application running locally in three quick steps:</p>
<p><strong>1. Generate the Prisma Client:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> generate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --no-engine</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p><strong>2. View your database in Prisma Studio:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> run</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> db:studio</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Prisma Studio opens at <code>localhost:5555</code> where you can inspect your <code>User</code> table and see the test user stored in your database.</p>
<p><strong>3. Start your Next.js development server:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> run</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> dev</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Visit <code>http://localhost:3000</code> to see your Next.js application live, displaying your first user fetched directly from your Prisma Postgres database!</p></div><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4 border-t pt-6 text-sm"><a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"
